You can use a Bluetooth controller such as AirTurn’s BT-105/106 or BT200 or other similar controller to control music playback and switch to other music in a playlist. Plus, the player is able to display lyrics or transcripts in sync with the music such as backing tracks.\r\n\r\nOperations are very simple. There are only two commands: File and Test signal. Click File command to select a folder that contains your music files (mp3, flac and wav) and lyrics files (.lrc or .srt). Refer to another app “LectureMate for Teachers’ for how to use lyrics files.\r\n\r\nAnother command is the Test signal. Before buying a Bluetooth controller you can use this command to test if a Bluetooth controller fits your needs.
